FNV VOLUMETRIC SHADOW TEXTURE LIFECYCLE FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

Proven starting point:
1. B9FDA0 constructs the 0x250-byte per-light shadow object and initializes +0x10C to null.
2. B5B1F0/B5B060/B5C3C0 release the refcounted +0x10C resource.
3. B9F780 renders the selected light offscreen and dispatches ImageSpace effect 0x11 with +0x10C.

Closure questions:
1. Which exact instruction writes the live +0x10C rendered texture, and with what creation/borrow parameters?
2. Is +0x10C the raw shadow map, a filtered copy, or another image-space intermediate?
3. Which shader texture slot consumes it, and how does that slot map to each selected light?
4. What dimensions, D3D format, depth surface, projection matrix, and frame lifetime apply?
5. What is rendered-texture type 0x2D in the RenderShadowMaps tail, and is it related to +0x10C?

Scope guard:
Field-offset scanning is restricted to the proven RenderShadowMaps, shadow manager, rendered-texture manager, and shadow/image-space bridge ranges. It is not a whole-program layout inference.
